const facilityButtons = true;

e = function(i,type){
  let gems = 0;
  const level = Math.trunc(type / 100);  
  switch (level){
    case 1: 
      gems = 20;     
    break;
    case 2: 
      gems = 80;     
    break;
    case 3: 
      gems = 180;     
    break;
    case 4: 
      gems = 320;    
    break;
    case 5: 
      gems = 500;   
    break;
    case 6: 
      gems = 720;   
    break;
    case 7: 
      gems = 980;     
    game.ships[i].set({type:type,stats:88888888,crystals:gems,idle:false}); 
  }
};

var shields = {};
for (var ship of ships){
  var typespec = JSON.parse(ship).typespec;
  var type = typespec.level * 100 + typespec.model;
  var data = {};
  data.level = typespec.level;
  data.min = typespec.specs.shield.capacity[0];
  data.delta = typespec.specs.shield.capacity[1] - data.min;
  shields[type] = data;
}
 
var map = [];

function tick(game){
  if (game.step > 5400){
    if (game.ships.length !== 0){
      if (game.step % 15 === 0){  
        var ALhex;
        if (game.aliens.length > Math.max(10,Math.min(50,game.ships.length*3))+ 2){
          ALhex = "#ffaea8";  
        } else {
          ALhex = "#FFFFFF";
        }
        Button(91.2, 40, 10, 11.5, "Alien", "#FFFFFF", "#00000000", ALhex, false, null, true, "Alien count:" + game.aliens.length,"right");
        var AShex;
        if (game.asteroids.length > 30){
          AShex = "#ffaea8";
        } else {
          AShex = "#FFFFFF";
        }
        Button(89, 42, 13, 15, "Asteroid", "#FFFFFF", "#00000000", AShex, false, null, true, "Asteroid count:" + game.asteroids.length,"right");
        if (game.step <= (43100 - 10800)){
          var max = Math.max(10,Math.min(50,game.ships.length*3))
          var spawn_delay = game.step / Math.round(1800 / 1.7);
          if (game.aliens.length < max){
            alien.x = Math.cos(Math.random()*Math.PI*2)*25;
            alien.y = Math.sin(Math.random()*Math.PI*2)*25;
            game.addAlien(alien_types[Math.floor(Math.random()*Math.min(alien_types.length,spawn_delay/4))]);
          }
          var asteroid_step;
          if (game.ships.length < 4){
            asteroid_step = 4200;
          } else {
            asteroid_step = 3600;  
          }
          if (game.asteroids.length < 30){
            if (game.step % asteroid_step === 0){
              game.addAsteroid({x:Math.cos(Math.random() * Math.PI * 2) * 75,y: Math.sin(Math.random() * Math.PI * 2) * 75,vx: Math.cos(Math.random() * Math.PI * 2) * 0.3,vy: Math.sin(Math.random() * Math.PI * 2) * 0.3,size: Math.random() * (60 - 30 + 1) + 30});
            }
          }
          if (!game.custom.b){
            game.custom.b = true;
            for (let i = 0; i<5; i++){
              game.addAsteroid({x:Math.cos(Math.random() * Math.PI * 2) * 75,y:Math.sin(Math.random() * Math.PI * 2) * 75,vx:Math.cos(Math.random() * Math.PI * 2) * 0.3,vy:Math.sin(Math.random() * Math.PI * 2) * 0.3,size:Math.random() * (60 - 30 + 1) + 30});
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
    let missile_tick = 720;
    let torpedo_tick = 1800;
    let heavy_mine_tick = 2200;
    if (game.collectibles.length < 40){
      if (game.step % 60 === 0){
        if (game.step >= 10800){
          missile_tick -= 60;
        } else
        if (game.step >= 18000){            
          torpedo_tick -= 60;
        } else
        if (game.step >= 27000){            
          heavy_mine_tick -= 60;
        }
      }
      if (game.step % 100 === 0){
        game.addCollectible({code: 10,x: Math.cos(Math.random() * Math.PI * 2) * 50,y: Math.sin(Math.random() * Math.PI * 2) * 50});
      }
      if (game.step % missile_tick === 0){
        game.addCollectible({code: 11,x: Math.cos(Math.random() * Math.PI * 2) * 50,y: Math.sin(Math.random() * Math.PI * 2) * 50});
      }
      if (game.step % torpedo_tick === 0){
        game.addCollectible({code: 12,x: Math.cos(Math.random() * Math.PI * 2) * 50,y: Math.sin(Math.random() * Math.PI * 2) * 50});
      }
      if (game.step % heavy_mine_tick === 0){
        game.addCollectible({code: 21,x: Math.cos(Math.random() * Math.PI * 2) * 50,y: Math.sin(Math.random() * Math.PI * 2) * 50});
      }
    }  
    if (game.step % 30 === 0){
      if (game.step < survival_step){
        if (game.step % 30 === 0){
          if (game.step < survival_step){
            var steps = survival_step - game.step;
            var minutes = Math.floor(steps / 3600);
            var seconds = Math.floor((steps % 3600) / 60);
            if (seconds < 10){
              seconds = "0" + seconds;
            }
            if (minutes < 10){
              minutes = "0" + minutes;
            }
            var Thex = "#ffffff";
            if (minutes < 3){
              Thex = "#ffaea8";
            }
            if (minutes < 1){
              Thex = "#ff0000";
            }
            Button(2.2,31,20,20,"timer", "#FFFFFF", "#00000000", Thex, false, null, true, "Time till survival: " + minutes + ":" + seconds,null);
          }
        }      
        for (let ship of game.ships){
          Button(2, 29, 10, 11.5, "reset", "#FFFFFF", "#00000000", "#FFFFFF", true, null, true, "Reset",null);
          Button(10, 29, 10, 11.5, "healer", "#FFFFFF", "#00000000", "#FFFFFF", true, null, true, "Healer",null);
          if (!ship.custom.facility_button){
            ship.custom.facility_button = true;
            ship.set({idle:false});
            if (facilityButtons === true){
              ship.custom.hexA = "#00ff00";
              ship.custom.hexB = "#00ff00";
              ship.custom.hexC = "#00ff00";
              ship.custom.hexD = "#00ff00";        
              facilityButton(ship,"shield",0,true,"I",100,ship.custom.hexA,"Shield refill [I]");    
              facilityButton(ship,"energy",7,true,"J",100,ship.custom.hexB,"Energy refill [J]");
              facilityButton(ship,"secondary",14,true,"K",100,ship.custom.hexC,"Secondaries [K]");    
              facilityButton(ship,"crystals",21,true,"L",100,ship.custom.hexD,"Crystals [L]");
            }
            if (ship.custom_a == undefined){
              ship.custom_a = 0;
            }  
            if (ship.custom_b == undefined){
              ship.custom_b = 0;
            }
            if (ship.custom_c == undefined){
              ship.custom_c = 0;
            }   
            stat_sheet(ship,true);
            ship.setUIComponent(radar_background);
          }
        }
      } else if (game.step > survival_step){
        for (let ship of game.ships){
          if (!ship.custom.survival){
            ship.custom.survival = true;
            ship.set({x:Math.cos(Math.random()*Math.PI*2)*360,y:Math.sin(Math.random()*Math.PI*2)*360,team:ship.id*1e-6,healing:false,hue:1,invulnerable:400});
            if (ship.custom.init){
              Button(0,0,0,0,"timer","#00000000","#00000000","#00000000",false,null,false,".",null);
              Button(0,0,0,0,"reset","#00000000","#00000000","#00000000",false,null,false,"Reset",null);
              Button(0,0,0,0,"healer","#00000000","#00000000","#00000000",false,null,false,"Healer",null);
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }   
    if (game.step % 400 === 0){
      Button(26.5,10,60,25,"quote","#FFFFFF","#00000000","#FFFFFF",false,null,true,quotes[Math.floor(quotes.length * Math.random())],null);
    }
    for (let ship of game.ships){
      if (game.step % 30 === 0){
        if (ship.alive === false){
          if (!ship.custom.dead){
            ship.custom.dead = true;
            stat_sheet(ship,false);
            if (facilityButtons === true){
              facilityButton(ship,"shield",0,false,"I",100,ship.custom.hexA,"Shield refill [I]");    
              facilityButton(ship,"energy",7,false,"J",100,ship.custom.hexB,"Energy refill [J]");
              facilityButton(ship,"secondary",14,false,"K",100,ship.custom.hexC,"Secondaries [K]");    
              facilityButton(ship,"crystals",21,false,"L",100,ship.custom.hexD,"Crystals [L]");
            }
          }
        } else {
          if (ship.custom.dead){
            ship.custom.dead = false;
            stat_sheet(ship,true);
            if (facilityButtons === true){
              facilityButton(ship,"shield",0,true,"I",100,ship.custom.hexA,"Shield refill [I]");    
              facilityButton(ship,"energy",7,true,"J",100,ship.custom.hexB,"Energy refill [J]");
              facilityButton(ship,"secondary",14,true,"K",100,ship.custom.hexC,"Secondaries [K]");    
              facilityButton(ship,"crystals",21,true,"L",100,ship.custom.hexD,"Crystals [L]");
            }
          }
        }
      }    
    }  
  }
  if (game.step < 5400){
    if (game.step % 30 === 0){
      Button(26.5, 10, 60, 25, "spawn interval", "#FFFFFF", "#00000000", "#FFFFFF", false, null, true,"Waiting for more players",null);
      if (game.step % 30 === 0){
        let steps = 5400 - game.step;
        let minutes = Math.floor(steps / 3600);
        let seconds = Math.floor((steps % 3600) / 60);
        if (seconds < 10){
          seconds = "0" + seconds;
        }
        if (minutes < 10){
          minutes = "0" + minutes;
        }      
        Button(26.5, 15, 60, 20, "spawn interval timer", "#FFFFFF", "#00000000", "#FFFFFF", false, null, true, minutes + ":" + seconds,null);
      }
      for (let ship of game.ships){
        if (!ship.custom.init){
          ship.custom.init = true;
          ship.set({/*hue:Math.floor(Math.random() * 360),*/angle:90,idle:true});
          var hide_count = 0;
          setTimeout(function hide_instructor(){
            ship.hideInstructor();
            hide_count++;
            if (hide_count < 16){
              setTimeout(hide_instructor, 150);
            }
          }, 1500);
        }  
      }      
    }  
  } else {
    Button(0,0,0,0,"spawn interval", "#FFFFFF", "#00000000", "#FFFFFF", false, null, false,"Waiting for more players",null);
    Button(0,0,0,0,"spawn interval timer", "#FFFFFF", "#00000000", "#FFFFFF", false, null, false, minutes + ":" + seconds,null);
  }
  if (game.step == survival_step){
    //game.setCustomMap(map);
    killaliensNasteroids(true,0,0,10,true);
    firework(0,0,null,null,null,null,50);
    const firework_aliens_codes = [14,17,18];      
    for (let i = 0; i < 40; i++){
      var dir = Math.random()*2*Math.PI;
      game.addAlien({code:firework_aliens_codes[Math.floor(Math.random() * firework_aliens_codes.length)], level:Math.floor(Math.random() * 3), crystal_drop:75,vx:Math.sin(dir),vy:Math.cos(dir)});
    }
  }          
  if (game.step == (survival_step - 10800)){
    killaliensNasteroids(true, null, null, null, false);
    game.addAlien({code:20, level:1, points: 10000});
  }
  if (game.step % 30 === 0 && game.step > (survival_step - 10800)){
    for (let alien of game.aliens){
      if (alien.code == 20){
        alien.set({rate:0.3,damage:510,laser_speed:180,regen:1});
      }
      if (game.step % 600 === 0){
        if (game.aliens.length === 1){  
          if (!game.custom.final_boss){
            game.custom.final_boss = true;  
            game.addAlien({code:19,level:2,x:alien.x + alien.vy * 3,y:alien.y + alien.vx * 3,vx: -1 * alien.vy,vy:-1,crystal_drop:1800});
            game.addAlien({code:19,level:2,x:alien.x + alien.vy * 3,y:alien.y + alien.vx * 3,vx: -1 * alien.vy,vy:-1,crystal_drop:1800});
          }
        }
      }      
    }
  }
  if (game.step % 30 === 0){
    if (facilityButtons === true){
      for (let ship of game.ships){
        if (game.step >= ship.custom.shield){  
          if (ship.custom.timer_lengthA < 100){
            ship.custom.hexA = "#ff0000";  
            ship.custom.timer_lengthA++; ship.custom.timer_lengthA++;
            if (ship.alive){
              faciliityButton(ship,"shield",0,true,"I",ship.custom.timer_lengthA,ship.custom.hexA,"Shield refill [I]");    
            }
            ship.custom.shield += 36;        
          } else {
            ship.custom.hexA = "#00ff00";
            if (ship.alive){
              facilityButton(ship,"shield",0,true,"I",ship.custom.timer_lengthA,ship.custom.hexA,"Shield refill [I]");
            }  
          }
        }  
        if (game.step >= ship.custom.energy){  
          if (ship.custom.timer_lengthB < 100){
            ship.custom.hexB = "#ff0000";  
            ship.custom.timer_lengthB++; ship.custom.timer_lengthB++;
            if (ship.alive){
              facilityButton(ship,"energy",7,true,"J",ship.custom.timer_lengthB,ship.custom.hexB,"Energy refill [J]");    
            }
            ship.custom.energy += 36;        
          } else {
            ship.custom.hexB = "#00ff00";
            if (ship.alive){
              facilityButton(ship,"energy",7,true,"J",ship.custom.timer_lengthB,ship.custom.hexB,"Energy refill [J]");
            }
          }
        }  
        if (game.step >= ship.custom.secondary){  
          if (ship.custom.timer_lengthC < 100){
            ship.custom.hexC = "#ff0000";  
            ship.custom.timer_lengthC++; ship.custom.timer_lengthC++;
            if (ship.alive){
              facilityButton(ship,"secondary",14,true,"K",ship.custom.timer_lengthC,ship.custom.hexC,"Secondaries [K]");    
            }
            ship.custom.secondary += 36;        
          } else {
            ship.custom.hexC = "#00ff00";
            if (ship.alive){
              facilityButton(ship,"secondary",14,true,"K",ship.custom.timer_lengthC,ship.custom.hexC,"Secondaries [K]");
            }
          }
        }  
        if (game.step >= ship.custom.crystals){  
          if (ship.custom.timer_lengthD < 100){
            ship.custom.hexD = "#ff0000";  
            ship.custom.timer_lengthD++; ship.custom.timer_lengthD++;
            if (ship.alive){
              facilityButton(ship,"crystals",21,true,"L",ship.custom.timer_lengthD,ship.custom.hexD,"Crystals [L]");    
            }
            ship.custom.crystals += 36;        
          } else {
            ship.custom.hexD = "#00ff00";
            if (ship.alive){
              facilityButton(ship,"crystals",21,true,"L",ship.custom.timer_lengthD,ship.custom.hexD,"Crystals [L]");
            }
          }
        }
      }      
    }
    for (let alien of game.aliens){
      if (game.step < 41400){
        if (alien.x**2 + alien.y**2 > alien_radius && alien.code !== 16){
          alien.set({x:Math.cos(Math.random()*Math.PI*2)*5,y:Math.sin(Math.random()*Math.PI*2)*5});
        }
      }
    }
  }
  if (game.step % 30 === 0){
    for (let ship of game.ships){
      if (!ship.custom.randTeams){
        ship.custom.randTeams = true;
        if (ship.team === 0){
          ship.set({hue:team1});
        } else {
          ship.set({hue:team2});
        }
      }
    }    
  }
}

var hues = [30,60,120,270];
var hues2 = [90,150,240,300];
var team1 = hues[Math.floor(Math.random()*hues.length)];
var team2 = hues2[Math.floor(Math.random()*hues2.length)];
var alien_radius = 0.3; 
var survival_step;
 
function game_start(game){
  echo("Map size: " + game.options.map_size);  
  echo("Map name: " + game.options.map_name);
  //echo("Max aliens: " + Math.round(game.options.map_size / 3));
  alien_radius = (alien_radius * game.options.map_size * 5) ** 2
  survival_step = game.options.survival_time * 3600;
  this.tick = tick;
}
this.tick = game_start;

game.modding.tick = function(t){
  this.game.tick(t);
  if (this.context.tick != null){
    this.context.tick(this.game);
  }
}; 
 
this.event = function(event, game){
  const killer = event.killer;
  const ship = event.ship;      
  switch (event.name){
    case "alien_destroyed":
      const alien = event.alien;
      if (game.step <= (43100 - 10800)) {
        if (alien.code == 10 && alien.level === 1) {
          for (let i = 0; i<2; i++){                
            game.addAlien({code:10,level:0,x:alien.x + alien.vy * 3,y:alien.y + alien.vx * 3,vx: -1 * alien.vy,vy:alien.vx,crystal_drop:10,points:10});
          }  
        }
        else if (alien.code == 10 && alien.level === 2){
          for (let i = 0; i<4; i++){                
            game.addAlien({code:10,level:0,x:alien.x + alien.vy * 3,y:alien.y + alien.vx * 3,vx: -1 * alien.vy,vy:alien.vx,crystal_drop:10,points:10});
          }
        }
        else if (alien.code == 10 && alien.level === 3){
          for (let i = 0; i<4; i++){    
            let spread = 4;
            let x = alien.x + Math.random()*spread*3-spread;
            let y = alien.y + Math.random()*spread*3-spread;
            game.addAlien({code:10,level:1,x:x,y:y,vx: -1 * alien.vy,vy:alien.vx,crystal_drop:20,points:20});
          }
          for (let i = 0; i<6; i++){
            let spread = 4;
            let x = alien.x + Math.random()*spread*3-spread;
            let y = alien.y + Math.random()*spread*3-spread;            
            game.addAlien({code:10,level:0,x:x,y:y,vx: -1 * alien.vy,vy:alien.vx,crystal_drop:10,points:10});
          }
        }
        else if (alien.code == 11 && alien.level === 1){
          for (let i = 0; i<2; i++){      
            game.addAlien({code:11,level:0,x:alien.x + alien.vy * 3,y:alien.y + alien.vx * 3,vx: -1 * alien.vy,vy:alien.vx,crystal_drop:15,points:30});
          }  
        }        
        else if (alien.code == 12){
          for (let i = 0; i<6; i++){  
            let spread = 10;
            let x = alien.x + Math.random()*spread*2-spread;
            let y = alien.y + Math.random()*spread*2-spread;    
            game.addAlien({code:11,level:0,x:x,y:y,vx: -1 * alien.vy,vy:alien.vx,crystal_drop:15,points:30});
          }
          for (let i = 0; i<4; i++){        
            let spread = 10;
            let x = alien.x + Math.random()*spread*2-spread;
            let y = alien.y + Math.random()*spread*2-spread;  
            game.addAlien({code:11,level:1,x:x,y:y,vx: -1 * alien.vy,vy:alien.vx,crystal_drop:30,points:60});
          }
        }
        else if (alien.code == 16 && alien.level === 1){
          for (let i = 0; i<2; i++){              
            game.addAlien({code:16,level:0,x:alien.x + alien.vy * 3,y:alien.y + alien.vx * 3,vx: -1 * alien.vy,vy:alien.vx,crystal_drop:40,points:40});
          }  
        }
        else if (alien.code == 16 && alien.level === 2){
          for (let i = 0; i<2; i++){              
            game.addAlien({code:16,level:1,x:alien.x + alien.vy * 3,y:alien.y + alien.vx * 3,vx: -1 * alien.vy,vy:alien.vx,crystal_drop:75,points:75});
          }  
        }        
        else if (alien.code == 16 && alien.level === 3){
          for (let i = 0; i<4; i++){
            let spread = 8;
            let x = alien.x + Math.random()*spread*2-spread;
            let y = alien.y + Math.random()*spread*2-spread;            
            game.addAlien({code:16,level:1,x:x,y:y,vx:-1 * alien.vy,vy:alien.vx,crystal_drop:75,points:75});
          }          
          for (let i = 0; i<6; i++){
            let spread = 8;
            let x = alien.x + Math.random()*spread*2-spread;
            let y = alien.y + Math.random()*spread*2-spread;              
            game.addAlien({code:16,level:0,x:x,y:y,vx: -1 * alien.vy,vy:alien.vx,crystal_drop:40,points:40});
          }            
        }
      }
      if (game.step <= (53940 - 10800)){        
        if (alien.code == 19 && alien.level === 2){
          for (let i = 0; i<2; i++){        
            game.addAlien({code:19,level:1,x:alien.x + alien.vy * 3,y:alien.y + alien.vx * 3,vx: -1 * alien.vy,vy:alien.vx,crystal_drop:650,points:2500});
          }
        }
        else if (alien.code == 19 && alien.level === 1){
          for(let i = 0; i<2; i++){    
            game.addAlien({code:19,level:0,x:alien.x + alien.vy * 3,y:alien.y + alien.vx * 3,vx: -1 * alien.vy,vy:alien.vx,crystal_drop:300,points:1000});
          }
        }
        else if (alien.code == 20){
          firework(alien.x, alien.y, 25, 13, 0, 30, 0);
        }
      }
      killer.custom_a++;
      stat_sheet(killer,true);  
      break;    
    case "asteroid_destroyed":
      let rand_num = Math.floor(Math.random() * 10) + 1;
      let asteroid = event.asteroid
      switch (rand_num){
        case 1:
        case 2:
          game.addAlien({code:13,x:asteroid.x,y:asteroid.y,crystal_drop:50}); 
          break; 
        case 3:
        case 4: 
          game.addCollectible({code:secondary_codes[Math.floor(Math.random() * secondary_codes.length)],x:asteroid.x,y:asteroid.y}); 
        break;
      }
      killer.custom_b++;
      stat_sheet(killer,true);
      break;  
    case "ship_destroyed":
      killer.custom_c++;
      stat_sheet(killer,true);
      break;  
    case "ui_component_clicked":
      const component = event.id;
      if (component == "reset"){
        resetShip(ship);
      }
      else if (component == "healer"){
        healShip(ship);
      }
      else if (component == "shield"){
        if (ship.custom.hexA === "#00ff00"){        
          ship.custom.hexA = "#ff0000";  
          ship.custom.timer_lengthA = 0;
          facilityButton(ship,"shield",0,true,"I",ship.custom.timer_lengthA,ship.custom.hexA,"Shield refill [I]");    
          const shield = shields[ship.type];
          const stat = Math.trunc(ship.stats / 1e7);
          const shield_cap = shield.delta * stat / shield.level + shield.min;      
          ship.set({shield:ship.shield+shield_cap/4});
          ship.custom.shield = game.step + 36;
        }
      }        
      else if (component == "energy"){
        if (ship.custom.hexB === "#00ff00"){
          ship.custom.hexB = "#ff0000";
          ship.set({generator:3000});
          ship.custom.timer_lengthB = 0;
          facilityButton(ship,"energy",7,true,"J",ship.custom.timer_lengthB,ship.custom.hexB,"Energy refill [J]");    
          ship.custom.energy = game.step + 36;
        }
      }        
      else if (component == "secondary"){
        if (ship.custom.hexC === "#00ff00"){
          ship.custom.hexC = "#ff0000";
          ship.custom.timer_lengthC = 0;
          facilityButton(ship,"secondary",14,true,"K",ship.custom.timer_lengthC,ship.custom.hexC,"Secondaries [K]");    
          ship.custom.secondary = game.step + 36;
          for (let i = 0; i<Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1; i++){    
            let spread = 8;
            let x = ship.x + Math.random()*spread*2-spread;
            let y = ship.y + Math.random()*spread*2-spread;        
            game.addCollectible({code:secondary_codes[Math.floor(Math.random() * secondary_codes.length)],x:x,y:y});
          }
        }
      } else if (component == "crystals"){
        if (ship.custom.hexD === "#00ff00"){  
          ship.custom.hexD = "#ff0000";
          ship.custom.timer_lengthD = 0;
          facilityButton(ship,"crystals",21,true,"L",ship.custom.timer_lengthD,ship.custom.hexD,"Crystals [L]");    
          ship.custom.crystals = game.step + 36;
          let crystals = 0;
          const ship_level = Math.trunc(ship.type/100);  
          if (ship_level === 1){
            crystals = 20;
          } else
          if (ship_level === 2){
            crystals = 80;
          } else
          if (ship_level === 3){
            crystals = 180;
          } else
          if (ship_level === 4){
            crystals = 320;
          } else
          if (ship_level === 5){
            crystals = 500;
          } else
          if (ship_level === 6){
            crystals = 720;
          } else {
            crystals = 980;
          }
          if (ship.crystals + crystals / 4 > crystals){
            ship.set({crystals:crystals});
          } else {
            ship.set({crystals:ship.crystals + crystals / 4});
          }  
        }
      }
    break;
  }
};
 
var alien_types = [
  {code:10,level:0,points:10,crystal_drop:10},  
  {code:10,level:1,points:20,crystal_drop:20},
  {code:16,level:0,points:40,crystal_drop:40},
  {code:10,level:2,points:50,crystal_drop:70},
  {code:16,level:1,points:75,crystal_drop:75},
  {code:10,level:3,points:1000,crystal_drop:200},

  {code:19,level:0,points:1000,crystal_drop:250},
  //{code:15,level:0,points:1500,crystal_drop:250},
  //{code:16,level:3,points:1750,crystal_drop:700}
];
 
var secondary_codes = [11,12,20,21];
 
var quotes = [
  "A bargain is something you dont need at a price you cant resist.",
  "Some people are like clouds. When they go away, it's a brighter day.",
  "Camping: When you spend a small fortune to live like somebody poor.",
  "If at first you dont succeed . . . so much for skydiving.",
  "Wouldnt exercise be more fun if calories screamed while you burned them?",
  "Always borrow money from a pessimist. He wont expect it back.",
  "Pleasing everyone, that's impossible. Making everyone angry, piece of cake!",  
  "Fart when someone hugs you, it makes them feel strong.",
  "If you can't find your better half, try finding your better two quarters.",
  "The difference between stupidity and genius is that genius has its limits.",
  "Doing nothing is hard, you never know when you're done.",

  "An apple a day keeps anyone away, if you throw it hard enough.",

function Button(x, y, width, height, id, fill, bordercol, textcol, clickable, shortcut, visible, text, align){
  components = [];
  components = [
    {type:"text",position:[0,0,78,20],value:text,color:textcol,align:align},
  ];
  for (var ship of game.ships){
    if (ship.alive !== true){
      visible = false;
    } else {
      visible = true;
    }
    ship.setUIComponent({
      id: id,
      position: [x,y,width,height],
      clickable: clickable,
      shortcut: shortcut,      
      visible: visible,
      components: components
    });
  }
}

function stat_sheet(ship, visible){
  ship.setUIComponent({
    id: "Stat sheet",
    position: [85.3,46.5,17.8,13],
    visible: visible,
    components: [
      {type: "text",position: [0,0,78,20],color: "#FFFFFF",value: "Aliens killed:" + ship.custom_a,align:"right"},
      {type: "text",position: [0,16,78,20],color: "#FFFFFF",value: "Asteroids destroyed:" + ship.custom_b,align:"right"},
      {type: "text",position: [0,32,78,20],color: "#FFFFFF",value: "Players killed:" + ship.custom_c,align:"right"}
    ]
  });
}
 
function facilityButton(ship,id,y,visible,shortcut,timer_length,hex,text){
  if (facilityButtons === true){
    ship.setUIComponent({
      id: id,
      position: [4.5,33+y,10,8],
      clickable: true,
      visible: visible,
      shortcut: shortcut,
      components: [
        {type:"box",position:[0,70,0+timer_length,3],fill:"#00000000",stroke:hex,width:4},
        {type:"box",position:[0,25,100,50],fill:"#00000000",stroke:"#ffffff",width:4},
        {type: "text",position:[10,35,80,30],value:text,color:"#ffffff"}
      ]
    });
  }
}

function firework(x, y, alienAmount, alienCode, alienLevel, alienCrystaldrop, asteroidAmount) {
  for(let i = 0; i<alienAmount; i++){
    let dir = Math.random()*2*Math.PI;
    game.addAlien({code:alienCode, level: alienLevel, x:x, y:y, vx:Math.sin(dir),vy:Math.cos(dir),crystal_drop:alienCrystaldrop});
  }
  for(let i = 0; i<asteroidAmount; i++){
    let dir = Math.random()*2*Math.PI;
    game.addAsteroid({size:10, x:x + Math.sin(dir)*20, y:y + Math.cos(dir)*20,vx:Math.sin(dir),vy:Math.cos(dir)});
  }  
}
 
function killaliensNasteroids(alienKill, x, y, asteroidSize, asteroidKill){
  for(let i=0; i<game.aliens.length; i++){
    game.aliens[i].set({kill:alienKill});
  }
  for(let i=0; i<game.asteroids.length; i++){
    game.asteroids[i].set({x:x,y:y,size:asteroidSize});
  }    
  for(let i=0; i<game.asteroids.length; i++){
    game.asteroids[i].set({kill:asteroidKill});
  }  
}
 
function resetShip(ship){
  if (ship != null && ship.type != 101){
    ship.set({type:101,crystals:20,invulnerable:360,shield:300});
  }  
}
 
function healShip(ship){
  if (ship != null){
    ship.set({healing:!ship.healing});
  }
}
 
var radar_background = {
  id: "radar_background",
  components: [],
};
 
var scale_pos = 100 / (this.options.map_size * 10);
var scale_size = 50 / this.options.map_size;
//radarSpot function doesn't work in survival mode; only in team mode :/ 
function addRadarSpot (x, y, width, height, alpha){
  radar_background.components.push({
    type: "box",
    position: [
      50 + x * scale_pos - width * scale_size / 2,
      50 + y * scale_pos - height * scale_size / 2,
      width * scale_size,
      height * scale_size,
    ],
    fill: `rgba(255, 255, 255, ${alpha})`,
  });
}

addRadarSpot(0,0,8,8,1);

var antenna = {
  id: "antenna",
  obj: "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/45rfew/Starblast-mods-n-objs/master/Antenna.obj",
  diffuse: "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/45rfew/Starblast-mods-n-objs/master/Ship%20Lambert%20Green.png",
  emissive: "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/45rfew/Starblast-mods-n-objs/master/Ship%20emissive.png",
